\DoxyCodeLine{883       \textcolor{comment}{// JavaScript 'null' is an Oddball that results in +0 when truncated to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{884       \textcolor{comment}{// Number. In a context like -\/0 == null, which must evaluate to false,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{885       \textcolor{comment}{// this truncation must not happen. For this reason we restrict this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{886       \textcolor{comment}{// case to when either the user explicitly requested a float (and thus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{887       \textcolor{comment}{// wants +0 if null is the input) or we know from the types that the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{888       \textcolor{comment}{// input can only be Number | Hole. The latter is necessary to handle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{889       \textcolor{comment}{// the operator CheckFloat64Hole. We did not put in the type (Number |}}
